```mermaid
flowchart TD
    Start[Component Mounts] --> FetchSub[fetchSubscription]
    FetchSub --> CheckMode{subscriptionDetails exists?}
    CheckMode -->|Yes| UpdateMode[mode = UPDATE]
    CheckMode -->|No| SaveMode[mode = SAVE]
    UpdateMode --> InitLocal[Initialize subscriptionLocal with existing data]
    SaveMode --> InitLocal
    InitLocal --> UserInteract[User Interacts with Form]
    UserInteract --> CheckEmail{Enable Email?}
    CheckEmail -->|Yes| ValidateEmail{Valid Email?}
    CheckEmail -->|No| CheckSMS
    ValidateEmail -->|Invalid| EmailError[isEmailSubscriptionInvalid = true]
    ValidateEmail -->|Valid| CheckSMS
    EmailError --> CheckSMS
    CheckSMS{Enable SMS?}
    CheckSMS -->|Yes| ValidateSMS{Valid Phone?}
    CheckSMS -->|No| CheckPlatform
    ValidateSMS -->|Invalid| SMSError[isMobileSubscriptionInvalid = true]
    ValidateSMS -->|Valid| CheckPlatform
    SMSError --> CheckPlatform
    CheckPlatform{Enable Platform?}
    CheckPlatform --> CheckChanges{hasVinSubscriptionChanged?}
    CheckChanges -->|No| DisableSave[Disable Save Button]
    CheckChanges -->|Yes| CheckValidation{Any Validation Errors?}
    CheckValidation -->|Yes| DisableSave
    CheckValidation -->|No| EnableSave[Enable Save Button]
    EnableSave --> UserSave[User Clicks Save]
    UserSave --> ShowModal{Show Confirmation Modal}
    ShowModal --> UserConfirm{User Confirms?}
    UserConfirm -->|Yes| CheckModeAction{mode = SAVE or UPDATE?}
    UserConfirm -->|No| Cancel[Cancel]
    CheckModeAction -->|SAVE| CallSubscribe[subscribe API]
    CheckModeAction -->|UPDATE| CallUpdate[updateSubscription API]
    CallSubscribe --> OnFinish[onRequestFinished]
    CallUpdate --> OnFinish
    OnFinish --> ShowSuccess[Show Success Alert]
    ShowSuccess --> End[End]
    Cancel --> End
```

## Diagram 2

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> Loading: Component Mounts
    Loading --> Loaded: Subscription Fetched
    Loading --> Error: Fetch Error
    Error --> Loaded: Retry
    Loaded --> SaveMode: No Existing Subscription
    Loaded --> UpdateMode: Existing Subscription
    SaveMode --> Editing: User Modifies Form
    UpdateMode --> Editing: User Modifies Form
    Editing --> Invalid: Validation Error
    Editing --> Valid: All Fields Valid
    Invalid --> Editing: User Fixes Error
    Valid --> ConfirmingCreate: Click Save (SaveMode)
    Valid --> ConfirmingUpdate: Click Save (UpdateMode)
    ConfirmingCreate --> Saving: User Confirms
    ConfirmingCreate --> Editing: User Cancels
    ConfirmingUpdate --> Updating: User Confirms
    ConfirmingUpdate --> Editing: User Cancels
    Saving --> Success: API Success
    Saving --> Failed: API Error
    Updating --> Success: API Success
    Updating --> Failed: API Error
    UpdateMode --> ConfirmingDelete: Click Delete
    ConfirmingDelete --> Deleting: User Confirms Delete
    ConfirmingDelete --> Unsubscribing: User Confirms Unsubscribe
    ConfirmingDelete --> Editing: User Cancels
    Deleting --> Success: Delete Success
    Deleting --> Failed: Delete Failed
    Unsubscribing --> Success: Unsubscribe Success
    Unsubscribing --> Failed: Unsubscribe Failed
    Success --> [*]
    Failed --> Editing: Retry
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant User
    participant AlertMeForm
    participant Redux
    participant API
    User->>AlertMeForm: Opens Form
    AlertMeForm->>Redux: getUserPreferences
    Redux-->>AlertMeForm: preferredEmail, preferredMobileNumber
    AlertMeForm->>API: fetchSubscription(subscribeeDetails)
    API-->>AlertMeForm: subscriptionDetails
    AlertMeForm->>AlertMeForm: Initialize subscriptionLocal
    User->>AlertMeForm: Toggles enable_email
    AlertMeForm->>AlertMeForm: Update subscriptionLocal
    User->>AlertMeForm: Enters recipient_email
    AlertMeForm->>AlertMeForm: Validate email
    User->>AlertMeForm: Toggles enable_sms
    AlertMeForm->>AlertMeForm: Update subscriptionLocal
    User->>AlertMeForm: Enters mobile_number
    AlertMeForm->>AlertMeForm: Validate phone
    User->>AlertMeForm: Clicks Save
    AlertMeForm->>AlertMeForm: hasVinSubscriptionChanged()
    AlertMeForm->>User: Show Confirmation Modal
    User->>AlertMeForm: Confirms
    alt mode = SAVE
        AlertMeForm->>API: subscribe(subscribeeDetails, subscriptionLocal)
    else mode = UPDATE
        AlertMeForm->>API: updateSubscription(subscribeeDetails, subscriptionLocal)
    end
    API-->>AlertMeForm: Success/Error
    AlertMeForm->>AlertMeForm: setShowAlert(true)
    AlertMeForm->>User: Display Success/Error Alert
    alt User clicks Delete
        User->>AlertMeForm: Clicks Delete
        AlertMeForm->>User: Show Delete Confirmation Modal
        User->>AlertMeForm: Selects Delete or Unsubscribe and Delete
        alt Delete Only
            AlertMeForm->>API: deleteSubscription(subscribeeDetails)
        else Unsubscribe and Delete
            AlertMeForm->>API: unsubscribe(subscribeeDetails)
        end
        API-->>AlertMeForm: Success/Error
        AlertMeForm->>User: Display Result
    end
```

## Diagram 4

```mermaid
graph LR
    A[subscriptionLocal State] --> B{enable_email}
    B -->|true| C[recipient_email required]
    C --> D{isValidEmail?}
    D -->|false| E[isEmailSubscriptionInvalid = true]
    D -->|true| F[Valid]
    A --> G{enable_sms}
    G -->|true| H[mobile_number required]
    H --> I{isPossiblePhoneNumber?}
    I -->|false| J[isMobileSubscriptionInvalid = true]
    I -->|true| K[Valid]
    A --> L{enable_platform}
    E --> M[Disable Save Button]
    J --> M
    F --> N{hasVinSubscriptionChanged?}
    K --> N
    L --> N
    N -->|false| M
    N -->|true| O{isUnsubscription?}
    O -->|true| M
    O -->|false| P[Enable Save Button]
```
